[1m[95m# Agent:[00m [1m[92mDelivery Time-Based Route Planner[00m
[95m## Task:[00m [92mYou are given a set of validated delivery orders grouped by H3 index using the 'ClusterOrdersByGeoTool'. Each H3 cluster contains one or more delivery locations, and each location has one or more orders.

Your objective is to create initial delivery routes within each H3 cluster by organizing locations such that the **total estimated delivery time per route does not exceed 8 operational hours**.

Guidelines:
- For each H3 cluster, group delivery locations into one or more routes.
- Ensure that each route's total delivery time stays within the 8-hour limit.
- Minimize unnecessary splitting of locations across multiple routes, but allow it when delivery time constraints require.
- Do NOT mix locations from different H3 clusters in the same route.
- Do NOT perform fleet selection or weight/volume optimization in this step.

**Output**:
Return a JSON object containing:
- h3_index
- a list of location objects (locations) included in the route

Fleet assignment and load balancing will be handled in later stages.
**Return a valid compact JSON object. Do not wrap it in quotes.**[00m

[1m[95m# Agent:[00m [1m[92mRoute Time Optimizer[00m
[95m## Task:[00m [92mYou are given initial delivery routes clustered by H3 index but not yet optimized for time or weight constraints.

Use the 'EnrichClusteredOrders' tool to enrich these routes with accurate total weight and volume across all locations. Your task: First optimize these routes for time constraints:
- Delivery window: 08:00 AMâ€“05:00 PM (9 hours).
- Maximum total delivery time per route: **8 hours** (excluding breaks and travel overhead).
- Drivers may drive 4 hours maximum, then must take a 45-minute break.
- Peak hours (07:30â€“09:00, 16:30â€“18:30) increase travel time 1.5 and 1.7 times.

Splitting Rules:
- If total delivery time > 8 hours, **split** into multiple sub-routes.
- Split by grouping locations based on `est_delivery_time_hours`.
- **Only group locations from the same H3 index**.
- No mixing locations across different H3 indexes.
- No dropping locations.

Fleet Assignment Rules (Time Optimization Focus):
- Prefer smaller fleets for better time efficiency in most cases
- Consider that larger fleets may have longer loading/unloading times
- Use only available fleet IDs from the Fleet tool
- Reserve Large fleets only for:
  - Routes with many locations where consolidation saves significant time
  - Areas with known traffic bottlenecks
- Never assign a larger fleet unless it demonstrably improves time efficiency

Important:
- Fleet size affects both capacity and time efficiency
- Delivery time limits (max 8 hours) apply to all fleets equally.
- Larger fleets cannot deliver beyond the 8-hour window.

Strict Rules:
- No assumptions about package size, weight, or traffic uniformity.
- No route may exceed 8 delivery hours, weight, volume, or driving time limits.

**Return a properly structured TimeOptimisedRoutes object that includes all required fields for enrichment. Include a meaningful explanations with appropriate metrics.**[00m

[1m[95m# Agent:[00m [1m[92mFleet Weight Specialist[00m
[95m## Task:[00m [92mOptimize routes for weight constraints using fleet capabilities.
Key Rules:
1. Never exceed fleet weight capacities
2. Preserve existing time windows
3. Only adjust fleet assignments when necessary
Follow these rules absolutely:
- Use available fleet weight capacity limits from the 'FleetTool'.
- Do NOT exceed a fleet's maximum weight capacity under any circumstances
- Preserve time constraints - no route may exceed 8 delivery hours

Fleet Weight Capacity Evaluation:
- Small: 2000kg capacity
- Medium: 5000kg capacity
- Large: 10000kg capacity

Optimal Fleet Selection Rules:
1. First evaluate ALL possible fleet options that can handle the route's weight
2. Consider:
   * Fleet utilization efficiency
   * Available fleet inventory
   * Operational costs
3. Prefer:
   * Higher utilization (70-90% ideal)
   * Lower cost per kg
4. Only split routes when:
   * No available fleet can handle the weight
   * Significant efficiency gains possible
- Assign appropriate fleet considering:
  * Weight capacity requirements
  * Available fleet count per type
  * Future volume optimization needs
- Check fleet availability before assignment
- Volume optimization will happen in next stage - but consider likely volume needs
- You MAY redistribute locations between routes **within the same H3 index only**.
- Do NOT drop or ignore any location with valid orders.
- Priority orders (priority: true) must always be preserved in a valid route.
- Orders with inventory_issue: true must remain excluded.

If no improvement is possible for a route, retain it as is.

**Your response must be a valid JSON object. Do not wrap it in quotes. Include a meaningful explanations with appropriate metrics. **[00m

[1m[95m# Agent:[00m [1m[92mFleet Volume Specialist[00m
[95m## Task:[00m [92mFinal optimization for volume while preserving all time and weight decisions.
Key Rules:
1. Validate time and weight constraints first
2. Only adjust packing configurations
3. Never violate previous optimizations
- Use available fleet volume capacity limits from the 'FleetTool'.
- Do NOT exceed a fleet's maximum volume capacity under any circumstances
- Preserve weight and time constraints from previous optimizations

Fleet Volume Capacity Evaluation:
- Small: 10 cubic_meters capacity
- Medium: 20 cubic_meters capacity
- Large: 50 cubic_meters capacity

Optimal Fleet Selection Rules:
1. First evaluate ALL possible fleet options that can handle the route's volume
2. Consider:
   * Fleet utilization efficiency
   * Available fleet inventory
   * Operational costs
3. Prefer:
   * Higher utilization (70-90% ideal)
   * Lower cost per cubic_meter
4. Only split routes when:
   * No available fleet can handle the volume
   * Significant efficiency gains possible
- Assign appropriate fleet considering:
  * Volume capacity requirements
  * Available fleet count per type
  * Weight constraints from previous optimization
- Check fleet availability before assignment
- Include meaningful explanations with appropriate metrics.
